\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Load gene expression data}
\NormalTok{counts\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read.csv}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"C:/Users/lohit marla/Documents/RNAseq{-}Analysis/data/rna\_seq\_counts\_matrix.csv"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{row.names =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Load metadata}
\NormalTok{metadata\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read.csv}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"C:/Users/lohit marla/Documents/RNAseq{-}Analysis/conf/metadata.csv"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{row.names =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Ensure \textquotesingle{}type\textquotesingle{} column in metadata is a factor}
\NormalTok{metadata\_df}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{type }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{as.factor}\NormalTok{(metadata\_df}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{type)}

\CommentTok{\# Function to filter out unwanted genes}
\NormalTok{is\_unwanted\_gene }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(gene\_name) \{}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{grepl}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\^{}(GM|gm|Gm|IG|ig|Ig)"}\NormalTok{, gene\_name)) \{}
    \FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{tolower}\NormalTok{(gene\_name) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{endsWith}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"rik"}\NormalTok{)) \{}
    \FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  \FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\CommentTok{\# Apply the function to filter out unwanted genes}
\NormalTok{filtered\_counts\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ counts\_df[}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{sapply}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{rownames}\NormalTok{(counts\_df), is\_unwanted\_gene), ]}


\CommentTok{\# Ensure that the sample names match}
\NormalTok{common\_samples }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{intersect}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(filtered\_counts\_df), }\FunctionTok{rownames}\NormalTok{(metadata\_df))}
\NormalTok{filtered\_counts\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ filtered\_counts\_df[, common\_samples]}
\NormalTok{metadata\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ metadata\_df[common\_samples, ]}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Ensure p.adjust is numeric}
\NormalTok{go\_results}\SpecialCharTok{@}\NormalTok{result}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.adjust }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(go\_results}\SpecialCharTok{@}\NormalTok{result}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.adjust)}

\CommentTok{\# Get significant GO terms}
\NormalTok{significant\_go }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{subset}\NormalTok{(go\_results}\SpecialCharTok{@}\NormalTok{result, p.adjust }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}} \FloatTok{0.05}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Print significant GO terms}
\FunctionTok{print}\NormalTok{(significant\_go)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\FunctionTok{library}\NormalTok{(ggplot2)}

\CommentTok{\# Select top 10 enriched pathways}
\NormalTok{top\_go }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ significant\_go[}\DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{:}\DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{, ]}

\FunctionTok{ggplot}\NormalTok{(top\_go, }\FunctionTok{aes}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{x=}\FunctionTok{reorder}\NormalTok{(Description, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\FunctionTok{log10}\NormalTok{(p.adjust)), }\AttributeTok{y=}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\FunctionTok{log10}\NormalTok{(p.adjust))) }\SpecialCharTok{+}
  \FunctionTok{geom\_bar}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{stat=}\StringTok{"identity"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{fill=}\StringTok{"blue"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{+}
  \FunctionTok{coord\_flip}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{+}
  \FunctionTok{labs}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{title=}\StringTok{"Top 10 Enriched GO Terms"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{x=}\StringTok{"GO Term"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{y=}\StringTok{"{-}Log10 Adjusted P{-}Value"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{+}
  \FunctionTok{theme\_minimal}\NormalTok{()}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}
